#цепочка на пропаганду и ренейминг городов

country_event = { # Дело государствунной важности 
	id = rus_propaganda_and_reneim_event.1
	title = rus_propaganda_and_reneim_event.1.t
	desc = rus_propaganda_and_reneim_event.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_political_discussion
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = RUS
		RUS = { 
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = RUS_decabrists_not_in_power
			}
		}
		date > 1849.3.9 
	}
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rus_propaganda_and_reneim_event.1"
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rus_propaganda_and_reneim_event.1.a	
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				has_country_leader = { 
					name = RUS_Dmitry_Alekseevich_Milyutin 
					ruling_only = yes 
				} 
				
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -20
				has_country_leader = { 
					name = RUS_Konstantin_Nikolaevich 
					ruling_only = yes 
				} 
				
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -50
				has_country_leader = { 
					name = RUS_Mihail_Fedorovich_Orlov 
					ruling_only = yes 
				} 
				
			}
		}
		add_political_power = 25
		add_stability = -0.01
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rus_propaganda_and_reneim_event.1.b	
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				add = -5
				has_country_leader = { 
					name = RUS_Dmitry_Alekseevich_Milyutin 
					ruling_only = yes 
				} 
				
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 30
				has_country_leader = { 
					name = RUS_Konstantin_Nikolaevich 
					ruling_only = yes 
				} 
				
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 5
				has_country_leader = { 
					name = RUS_Mihail_Fedorovich_Orlov 
					ruling_only = yes 
				} 
				
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -25
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = rus_propaganda_and_reneim_event.2 days = 15 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rus_propaganda_and_reneim_event.1.c	
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				add = -100
				has_country_leader = { 
					name = RUS_Dmitry_Alekseevich_Milyutin 
					ruling_only = yes 
				} 
				
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -100
				has_country_leader = { 
					name = RUS_Konstantin_Nikolaevich 
					ruling_only = yes 
				} 
				
			}
			modifier = {
				add = 50
				has_country_leader = { 
					name = RUS_Mihail_Fedorovich_Orlov 
					ruling_only = yes 
				} 
				
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -50
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = rus_propaganda_and_reneim_event.2 days = 15 } #вызывает цепочку пропаганды
			country_event = { id = rus_propaganda_and_reneim_event.15 days = 7 } #вызывает цепочку ренейминга
		}
	}
	
}

			country_event = { id = rus_propaganda_and_reneim_event.5 days = 365 }	
			country_event = { id = rus_propaganda_and_reneim_event.10 days = 90 }		
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = authoritarian
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = authoritarian
					popularity = 0.05
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = reactionist
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = reactionist
					popularity = 0.05
				}
			}

				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}

	title = rus_propaganda_and_reneim_event.6.t
	desc = rus_propaganda_and_reneim_event.6.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_russian_deputies_miting
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rus_propaganda_and_reneim_event.6"	
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = authoritarian
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = authoritarian
					popularity = 0.025
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = reactionist
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = reactionist
					popularity = 0.025
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = democratic
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = 0.025
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rus_propaganda_and_reneim_event.6.a	
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				RUS = {
					has_idea = RUS_propaganda_in_press
				}
			}
			remove_ideas = RUS_propaganda_in_press
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_add_rulling_party_popularity
		custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_end_chain_propaganda_and_reneim_tt
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_political_power = 50
	}
	
}

	desc = russian_armed_forces_event.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_russian_millitary_planning

	fire_only_once = yes

		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event russian_armed_forces_event.2"
	}

		name = russian_armed_forces_event.2.a	
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_start_hidden_mobilisation
		hidden_effect = {
			add_timed_idea = {
				days = 365
				idea = RUS_hidden_mobilisation
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = {
						has_idea = extensive_conscription
					}
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = extensive_conscription
					add_idea = service_by_requirement
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = {
						has_idea = limited_conscription
					}
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = limited_conscription
					add_idea = extensive_conscription
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = {
						has_idea = volunteer_only
					}
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = volunteer_only
					add_idea = limited_conscription
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = {
						has_idea = disarmed_nation
					}
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = disarmed_nation
					add_idea = volunteer_only
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = russian_armed_forces_event.2.b	
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
	
}

	title = russian_european_politic.35.t
	desc = russian_european_politic.35.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_aotsm_generic_signing_the_contract
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event russian_european_politic.35"
	}
	
	option = {
		name = russian_european_politic.35.a	
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor  = 100
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		add_opinion_modifier = {
			target = RUS
			modifier = huge_increase
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			RUS = { country_event = { id = russian_european_politic.36 days = 3} }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = russian_european_politic.35.b	
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				factor  = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			RUS = { country_event = { id = russian_european_politic.37 days = 3} }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = russian_far_east_politic.1 #Претензии на приморский край
	title = russian_far_east_politic.1.t
	desc = russian_far_east_politic.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_russian_millitary_planning
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event russian_far_east_politic.1"
	}
	
	option = { 
		name = russian_far_east_politic.1.a	# Граница по Амуру - минимальный вариант - покупка земель - вероятнее всего дружба
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			RUS = { set_country_flag = RUS_china_far_east_small_plan }
			QIN = { country_event = { id = russian_far_east_politic.2 days = 2} }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = russian_far_east_politic.1.b	# Ханьшенвей наш - приморский край + Ханьшеньвей - дружеские отношения 50x50
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			RUS = { set_country_flag = RUS_china_far_east_medium_plan }
			QIN = { country_event = { id = russian_far_east_politic.5 days = 2 } }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = russian_far_east_politic.1.c	# Интервенция в маньчжурию - максимальный вариант  - контроль над Ханьшеньвенем и северной маньчжурией - дружба с Китаем невозможна
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
			}
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			RUS = { set_country_flag = RUS_china_far_east_big_plan }
			QIN = { country_event = { id = russian_far_east_politic.8 days = 2 } }
		}
	}
	
}

			base = 15
		}

			target = KAZ
			type = annex_everything
		}

					days = 90
					idea = RUS_conquer_central_asia_idea
				}
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					HIV = {
						is_in_faction_with = KAZ
					}
				}
				RUS = { set_country_flag = RUS_invasion_in_hiv_flag }
				add_to_war = {
					targeted_alliance = KAZ
					enemy = RUS
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					BUK = {
						is_in_faction_with = KAZ
					}
				}
				RUS = { set_country_flag = RUS_invasion_in_buk_flag }
				add_to_war = {
					targeted_alliance = KAZ
					enemy = RUS
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = russian_central_asia_politic.8.b #Мы не готовы

			base = 0
		}
		add_war_support = -0.05

	}

		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = RUS_give_finalnd_autonomy
		hidden_effect = {
			RUS = { set_country_flag = RUS_give_autonomy_finland }
			FIN = {
				transfer_state = 111
				transfer_state = 145
				transfer_state = 147
				transfer_state = 149
				transfer_state = 150
				set_cosmetic_tag = RUS_FIN
			}
			RUS = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = FIN
					autonomous_state = autonomy_colony
				}
			}
			FIN = {
				retire_country_leader = yes
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = authoritarian
					popularity = 0.30
				}
				set_politics = { ruling_party = authoritarian }
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = FIN_temporary_goverment
					promote_leader = yes

						expire = "1900.1.1"
						ideology = centrism
						traits = {  }
					}
				}
			}

		}
	}

				add_state_core = 111
				add_state_core = 145
				add_state_core = 147
				add_state_core = 149
				add_state_core = 150
			}
			111 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = RUS_integrated_finland_dynamic_modifier } }
			145 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = RUS_integrated_finland_dynamic_modifier } }
			147 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = RUS_integrated_finland_dynamic_modifier } }
			149 = { add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = RUS_integrated_finland_dynamic_modifier } }

country_event = {
	id = russian_socialist_political_event.6 # 
	title = russian_socialist_political_event.6.t
	desc = russian_socialist_political_event.6.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_aotsm_generic_signing_the_contract
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event russian_socialist_political_event.6"
	}
	
	option = {
		name = russian_socialist_political_event.6.a	
		add_political_power = 25	
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = RUS_country_save_market_economic
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = closed_economy
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = closed_economy
					add_idea = free_trade
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = limited_exports
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = limited_exports
					add_idea = free_trade
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = export_focus
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = export_focus
					add_idea = free_trade
				}
			}				
		}
	}
}

			}

				add_idea = RUS_soc_komission_on_national_minorities_problems
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			
		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = russian_socialist_trigger_event.1 # Свап оттока иностранного капитала 1
	title = russian_socialist_trigger_event.1.t
	desc = russian_socialist_trigger_event.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_aotsm_generic_signing_the_contract
	
	trigger = {
		tag = RUS
		has_idea = RUS_outflow_of_foreign_capital_1
		has_country_flag = {
			flag = RUS_outflow_of_foreign_capital_started
			days > 180
		}
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event russian_socialist_trigger_event.1"
	}
	
	option = {
		name = russian_socialist_trigger_event.1.a	
		
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = RUS_outflow_of_foreign_capital_1
			add_idea = RUS_outflow_of_foreign_capital_2
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			
		}
	}	

}

country_event = {
	id = russian_socialist_air_event.1 # Создание русской авиации
	title = russian_socialist_air_event.1.t
	desc = russian_socialist_air_event.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_aotsm_generic_signing_the_contract
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event russian_socialist_air_event.1"
	}
	
	option = {
		name = russian_socialist_air_event.1.a	
		air_experience = 10
		custom_effect_tooltip = air_base_build_rus_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = unlock_air_development_dec_flag
			set_temp_variable = {
				var = RUS.air_experience
				value = 0
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					RUS = {
						has_tech = iw_basic_airframe
					}
				}
				add_to_temp_variable = {
					var = RUS.air_experience
					value = 1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					RUS = {
						has_tech = aircraft_construction
					}
				}
				add_to_temp_variable = {
					var = RUS.air_experience
					value = 1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					RUS = {
						has_tech = iw_small_airframe
					}
				}
				add_to_temp_variable = {
					var = RUS.air_experience
					value = 1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					RUS = {
						has_tech = iw_medium_airframe
					}
				}
				add_to_temp_variable = {
					var = RUS.air_experience
					value = 1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					RUS = {
						has_tech = iw_large_airframe
					}
				}
				add_to_temp_variable = {
					var = RUS.air_experience
					value = 1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					RUS = {
						has_tech = early_bombs
					}
				}
				add_to_temp_variable = {
					var = RUS.air_experience
					value = 1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					RUS = {
						has_tech = aa_lmg
					}
				}
				add_to_temp_variable = {
					var = RUS.air_experience
					value = 1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					RUS = {
						has_tech = engines_1
					}
				}
				add_to_temp_variable = {
					var = RUS.air_experience
					value = 1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						RUS = {
							has_tech = aircraft_construction
						}
					}
				}
				RUS = {
					set_technology = {
						aircraft_construction = 1
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						RUS = {
							has_tech = iw_basic_airframe
						}
					}
				}
				RUS = {
					set_technology = {
						iw_basic_airframe = 1
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						RUS = {
							has_tech = iw_small_airframe
						}
					}
				}
				RUS = {
					set_technology = {
						iw_small_airframe = 1
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						RUS = {
							has_tech = iw_medium_airframe
						}
					}
				}
				RUS = {
					set_technology = {
						iw_medium_airframe = 1
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						RUS = {
							has_tech = iw_large_airframe
						}
					}
				}
				RUS = {
					set_technology = {
						iw_large_airframe = 1
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						RUS = {
							has_tech = early_bombs
						}
					}
				}
				RUS = {
					set_technology = {
						early_bombs = 1
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						RUS = {
							has_tech = aa_lmg
						}
					}
				}
				RUS = {
					set_technology = {
						aa_lmg = 1
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						RUS = {
							has_tech = engines_1
						}
					}
				}
				RUS = {
					set_technology = {
						engines_1 = 1
					}
				}
			}
			set_temp_variable = {
				var = RUS.air_experience_give
				value = 5
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						RUS.air_experience > 0
					}
				}
				multiply_temp_variable = { RUS.air_experience_give = RUS.air_experience }
				RUS = {
					air_experience = RUS.air_experience_give
				}
			}
		}
	}	

}

country_event = {
	id = russian_socialist_sphere_event.6 # Уничтожение агрессора - Ивент для Германии
	title = russian_socialist_sphere_event.6.t
	desc = russian_socialist_sphere_event.6.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_aotsm_generic_signing_the_contract
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event russian_socialist_sphere_event.6"
	}
	
	option = {
		name = russian_socialist_sphere_event.6.a #Не уступать	
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
		}
		RUS = {
			declare_war_on = {
				target = PRU
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_global_flag = wwi_russiansoc_attack_germany
			first_world_war_begin = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					BYZ = {
						is_in_faction_with = PRU
					}
				}
				BYZ = {
					add_to_war = {
						targeted_alliance = PRU
						enemy = RUS
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}	
	
	option = {
		name = russian_socialist_sphere_event.6.a #Уступить
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		trigger = {
			always = no #не проработано в принципе
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			
		}
	}	

}

			}
			add_to_variable = {

	picture = GFX_report_event_aotsm_generic_signing_the_contract
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event russian_socialist_sphere_event.52"
	}
	
	option = {
		name = russian_socialist_sphere_event.52.a	#
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {	
			if = {
				limit = {
					SCA = {
						owns_state = 148
					}
				}
				SCA = { country_event = { id = russian_socialist_sphere_event.53 days = 3 } }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					SWE = {
						owns_state = 148
					}
				}
				SWE = { country_event = { id = russian_socialist_sphere_event.53 days = 3 } }
			}
		}
	}	
	
	option = {
		name = russian_socialist_sphere_event.52.b	#
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
		}
		activate_mission = RUS_mission_intervention_in_scandinavy
		if = {
			limit = {
				SCA = { 
					#country_exists = yes
					owns_state = 148
				}
			}
			declare_war_on = {
				target = SCA
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				SWE = { 
					#country_exists = yes

country_event = {
	id = rus_leave_officers_event.2 # Исчезновение Игнатьева - для Пушкина и Герцена
	title = rus_leave_officers_event.2.t
	desc = rus_leave_officers_event.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_rus_topsecret
	
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = RUS
		RUS = { has_government = socialism }
		has_country_flag = {
			flag = RUS_start_leave_officers
			days > 28
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_leader = {
				character = RUS_Chernyshevskiy_Nikolay_Gavrilovich
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event rus_leave_officers_event.2"
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					RUS = { NOT = { has_country_flag = RUS_not_loyal_officers_purged } }
				}
				every_unit_leader = {
					limit = {
						has_trait = RUS_black_league
					}
					set_nationality = {
						target_country = RBL
					}
				}
				every_unit_leader = {
					limit = {
						has_trait = RUS_black_league_navy
					}
					set_nationality = {
						target_country = RBL
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = RUS_ignatiev_fade
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = rus_leave_officers_event.2.a	
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 15
		}
		
	}	
	
	option = {
		name = rus_leave_officers_event.2.b	#тут должна активироваться цепочка ивентов "Исчезновение Игнатьева" 
		
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		
		hidden_effect = {
			RUS = { country_event = { id = rus_rbl_uprising_event.1 days = 12 } }
		}	
	}	

}

		}

				transfer_state = 240
				transfer_state = 258
				transfer_state = 257
				transfer_state = 260
				add_state_core = 220
				add_state_core = 240
				add_state_core = 258
				add_state_core = 257
				add_state_core = 260
				load_oob = "RBL_uprising"
			}
			RBL = {
				inherit_technology = RUS
			}
			RBL = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					character = RUS_Pavel_Nikolaevich_Ignatiev
					promote_leader = yes
				
					country_leader = {

					ideology = reactionist
					portrait = GFX_rus_Pavel_Ignatiev_leader_rbl
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {

		ai_chance = {
			base = 15
		}

				}

		}
		if = {
			set_country_flag = RUS_td_neutral_end
		}
	}
